I feel that they really treat customers with care, and I am infected by this care and enthusiasm.
Room: For traveling with a baby, the area is not too big, the smart toilet is very convenient, the makeup mirror is good, the room is well soundproofed, and the room is close to the elevator entrance. I was worried that it would be too noisy and affect my sleep, but I found that it was completely fine. There is a slot, the bathroom is transparent glass, and there is no curtain to block it. When taking a shower in the bathroom, you can directly see the room. By the way, there are no electric curtains.
Buffet breakfast: There are not many varieties, but it is enough. It is in line with this price range of hotels.
Lunch: I ate a la carte dishes in the Chinese restaurant, fried rice, snail meat, and green pepper frog are all delicious.
Hot spring: It feels average, and I don‚Äôt feel that I need to pay for the hot spring.
Finally, the food and accommodation meet all my requirements for traveling with a baby. I originally planned to stay for only one night, but I stayed for three nights.
